We do our best to ensure that every patient has a positive experience when they come to see us, and take every complaint seriously.\n\nWe do have a strict policy regarding patient no-shows and same-day cancellations, because we want to ensure that our patients are able to see Dr. Enayati as soon as possible. If someone is not able to attend their appointment due to another commitment, we ask for at least 24 hours‚Äô notice so that we can offer that time to another patient. Dr. Enayati spends more time with each individual patient than most specialist doctors, so even a single patient no-show can leave a noticeable gap in our schedule‚Äì‚Äìtime that could have been given to another patient in need if we had enough notice. We hate telling someone who is suffering with pain that they need to wait for weeks to see Dr. Enayati and then have someone else not show up to their appointment that same day‚Äì‚Äìwe want to be able to give that slot to a person who needs and wants it! Although we do not enjoy charging late fees and no-show/late cancellation fees, we have found that charging a nominal fee is the most effective way to minimize wait times and ensure patient access to Dr. Enayati. All patients are notified about these policies when they first come to our office. < review>
Dr. Enayati is the most knowledgeable, caring pain management doctor I have ever met. I have suffered excruciating pain for 6 years after pushing a leg press that was too heavy.

Others doctors had no idea why the injury didn't heal after 4 to 6 weeks. They didn't believe how much pain I was in. I told told all the medical professionals that the pain was in an embarrassing area just to the left of my vulva and perineum and that sitting was extremely painful. None of them had heard of such a long-term condition in this area.

I went to physical therapy, had acupuncture, several cortisone shots, saw a chiropractor , all with no relief.  After 2 more years I was desperate saw an orthopedic surgeon. He misdiagnosed me, resected bone from my left femar and pelvic bone. My body reacted by creating a heterotopic ossification  (pemanent presence of bone in soft tissue where bone normally does not exist). He wanted to do the surgery again and remove even more bone when I told him the procedure was unsuccessful. I was afraid and did not go bavk.

The pain continued so I met with a pain management doctor near work. I told him as I had told everyone else had had several cordison shots asked for a nerve block. He instead gave me steroid injections two weeks apart. This was a waste of my money and time. Also, the shots were painful. I cried and he asked, haven't you had children before?" I hadn't and was embarrassed.

Just before the holidays 2017 I could no longer sit and do my job. I wasn't allowed a standing desk. I had to go on disability. I had been at my job for 16 years and whether people believed me or not I could no longer work.

I searched the internet and was willing to drive any distance for the right doctor.  After extensive research I found Dr. Enayati. He has saved me from a life of pain.

I first met with his medical assistant Peter. He was extremely thorough and compassionate with his questions.

Dr. Enayati came in the room after reading my medical history and Peter's notes. He ask, "Has anyone told you about Pudendal Neuropathy?" In the 6 years I searched for an answer no one had even mentioned it. A week later he did a diagnostic nerve block, totally painless, and confirmed that was my condition. He is now looking for the best surgeon to correct my injury. There are only a very few specilzed surgeons qualified to do it.

If you have pain, don't suffer for 6 years like I did. Make an appointment with Dr. Enayati. Also, his medical assistant Peter, office manager Craig and front desk manager Nany are all extremely good at their jobs and compassionate as well.< /review>

< review>
I like Forever 21 because it has a great fun choice of clothes for plus sizes and the prices are extremely reasonable. Plus size clothes are oftentimes unflattering but here they are fun and flattering. Employees are helpful and friendly. Two negative points are that it is EXTREMELY difficult to find good bargain clothes as they are only tragedy by color themes rather than by size . This makes shopping frustrating and irritating as you spend a ridiculous amount of time looking for the right sizes. On that end they need to rethink the concept to boost their sales. Their return policy is not good either as if you wear defective item and try to return it even after a few days, they will automatically refuse to take it back, only allowing exchanges or even exchanges. Many sale items are also FINAL sales..Fun store nonetheless to shop at...<//review>

We have been visiting this place for many years, since it's close by and convenient to place an order to go.  But as of last week, we will No Longer be spending our money there!
The owner was so Rude and Unkind to us, due to the fact that we ordered a pizza to go....and when we came to pick it up, we drove home to eat it with our family.
As we pulled the box top open, we quickly noticed that this pizza, cheese and crust were quite burnt!
It was definitely the color black on most of the pizza in which we ordered the largest size as we always do......
I called to let the staff know that we didn't take one bite of this pizza, and that could we have another one made up......
The owner who is a male, took over the conversation and asked for us to bring the pizza back, we did at that!
When we did bring it back without one bite on it, since we don't like the taste of blackened overcooked pizza,
the manager opened the pizza box and directly told us'
"Well, I really don't see why you brought this pizza back, most people would eat it black like this!!

That was very upsetting to my our family, we will never be back to this Pizza PLus!
It is worth the short drive to buy our pizzas elsewhere.....
So, I would suggest those who order pizzas to go that you take a peek inside first to make sure you don't have to drive back to get a better pizza made!
I don't recommend this certain establishment in Murphys, Ca!</review>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
I have been a long time customer at Tiki Lagun and have always appreciated the friendly staff. But this weekend the staff went above and beyond, for which I am very grateful!

There have been countless times that I have stopped to assist a boater in distress, and a lot of times that I have towed a disabled boat back to the marina.  Good Karma, I always thought.

But when it was my turn to be broken down do you think anyone stopped to offer me assistance?  Noooo!

Without many other options we called Tiki, told them where we were and in very short order Mark shows up with the Tiki boat and tows me back!

Mark, Shawn, and Mandy, thank you SO MUCH!

Rod McInnis<//Review>

The yelp reviews about this location tell it all...nice people at the front, but customer service, fulfillment of orders, follow-up, etc. is bad.  We ordered two Big Mac meals and asked for no pickles and extra sauce on both.  When we received our order, we were charged .49 cents for extra sauce, but the one burger that was marked extra sauce on the slip, had only a normal amount of sauce and the other was marked "no sauce" and had no sauce.   Why order something special if the order takers and/or preparers just ignore it?
We went back to the front and after being ignored repeatedly by the tall female server, the young man on the drive-up window came over and asked what we needed and got us some extra sauce. The tables were dirty throughout the restaurant and the french fry timer was constantly beeping during our entire time in the restaurant (and I mean constantly!).  Not sure if the staff were just ignoring it or if only one of them was authorized to TURN IT OFF!  A really bad experience overall here.  Multiple staff standing around, doing nothing...<//text>
